<div class="p-current-events-headlines" role="region" aria-labelledby="Topics&#95;in&#95;the&#95;news"><div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Topics_in_the_news">Topics in the news</h2></div><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1053378754">.mw-parser-output .itn-img{float:right;margin-left:0.5em;margin-top:0.2em}</style><div role="figure" class="itn-img">
<div class="thumbinner mp-thumb" style="background: transparent; color: inherit; border: none; padding: 0; max-width: 118px;">
<span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Lauren_Betts_(cropped).jpg" class="mw-file-description" title="Lauren Betts in 2026"><img alt="A woman in sports clothing" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Lauren_Betts_%28cropped%29.jpg/120px-Lauren_Betts_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="116" height="170" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Lauren_Betts_%28cropped%29.jpg/250px-Lauren_Betts_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1312" data-file-height="1919" /></a></span><div class="thumbcaption" style="padding: 0.25em 0; word-wrap: break-word; text-align: left;">Lauren Betts</div></div>

<ul><li>In <a href="/wiki/NCAA_Division_I" title="NCAA Division I">NCAA Division I</a> basketball, the <a href="/wiki/UCLA_Bruins_women%27s_basketball" title="UCLA Bruins women&#39;s basketball">UCLA Bruins</a> win <b><a href="/wiki/2026_NCAA_Division_I_women%27s_basketball_championship_game" title="2026 NCAA Division I women&#39;s basketball championship game">the women's championship</a></b> <i>(<a href="/wiki/NCAA_Division_I_basketball_tournament_Most_Outstanding_Player" title="NCAA Division I basketball tournament Most Outstanding Player">Most Outstanding Player</a> <a href="/wiki/Lauren_Betts" title="Lauren Betts">Lauren Betts</a> pictured)</i>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a>'s <b><a href="/wiki/Artemis_II" title="Artemis II">Artemis&#160;II</a></b> performs its lunar <a href="/wiki/Flyby_(spaceflight)" title="Flyby (spaceflight)">flyby</a> maneuver, becoming the farthest crewed mission from Earth.</li>
<li>In Mongolia, <b><a href="/wiki/Nyam-Osoryn_Uchral" title="Nyam-Osoryn Uchral">Nyam-Osoryn Uchral</a></b> is sworn in as <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Mongolia" title="Prime Minister of Mongolia">prime minister</a> following the resignation of <b><a href="/wiki/Gombojavyn_Zandanshatar" title="Gombojavyn Zandanshatar">Gombojavyn Zandanshatar</a></b>.</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Social_Democrats_(Denmark)" title="Social Democrats (Denmark)">Social Democrats</a>, led by Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Mette_Frederiksen" title="Mette Frederiksen">Mette Frederiksen</a>, remain the largest party after <b><a href="/wiki/2026_Danish_general_election" title="2026 Danish general election">the Danish general election</a></b>, with no political bloc winning a majority of seats.</li></ul>

    <div class="current-events-heading plainlinks">
        <div class="current-events-title" role="heading"><span class="summary">April&#160;8,&#160;2026<span style="display: none;">&#160;(<span class="bday dtstart published updated itvstart">2026-04-08</span>)</span> (Wednesday)</span>
        </div>
        <ul class="current-events-navbar editlink noprint"><li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2026_April_8&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></li><li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2026_April_8&amp;action=history">history</a></li><li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2026_April_8&amp;action=watch">watch</a></li>
        </ul>
    </div>
    <div class="current-events-content description">
<p><b>Armed conflicts and attacks</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iran_war" title="2026 Iran war">2026 Iran war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2025%E2%80%932026_Iran%E2%80%93United_States_negotiations" title="2025–2026 Iran–United States negotiations">2025–2026 Iran–United States negotiations</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Islamabad_Accord_(2026)" class="mw-redirect" title="Islamabad Accord (2026)">Islamabad Accord</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Iran)" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Iran)">Iranian foreign minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Abbas_Araghchi" title="Abbas Araghchi">Abbas Araghchi</a> confirms the two-week <a href="/wiki/Ceasefire" title="Ceasefire">ceasefire</a> between the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>, which includes reopening the <a href="/wiki/2026_Strait_of_Hormuz_crisis" title="2026 Strait of Hormuz crisis">Strait of Hormuz</a>. The ceasefire is ratified by the <a href="/wiki/Supreme_National_Security_Council" title="Supreme National Security Council">Supreme National Security Council</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://shafaq.com/en/Middle-East/Iran-agrees-to-ceasefire-offers-conditional-Hormuz-passage">(Shafaq)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.khaleejtimes.com/world/mena/iran-agrees-to-safe-passage-through-hormuz-strait-for-two-weeks-if-attacks-halted-2">(<i>Khaleej Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Supreme_National_Security_Council" title="Supreme National Security Council">Supreme National Security Council</a> says that negotiations between the United States and Iran will start on Friday in <a href="/wiki/Islamabad" title="Islamabad">Islamabad</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.middleeasteye.net/live-blog/live-blog-update/iran-says-talks-us-begin-friday-islamabad?topic=War%2520on%2520Iran&amp;id=436636&amp;fid=553792">(Middle East Eye)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel" title="Prime Minister of Israel">Israeli prime minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu" title="Benjamin Netanyahu">Benjamin Netanyahu</a> announces on social media that the ceasefire does not include <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/4/8/netanyahu-says-us-iran-ceasefire-does-not-include-lebanon">(Al Jazeera)</a></li>
<li>After the ceasefire took hold, <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> launches <a href="/wiki/Ballistic_missile" title="Ballistic missile">ballistic missiles</a> at Israel, Kuwait, Qatar, Bahrain, and the United Arab Emirates. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.cnbc.com/2026/04/08/iran-missile-attacks-after-us-ceasefire-gulf-air-defenses.html">(CNBC News)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>'s East-West oil pipeline is hit in an <a href="/wiki/Irani" class="mw-disambig" title="Irani">Iranian</a> attack. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/business/energy/saudi-arabias-east-west-oil-pipeline-hit-iranian-attack-damage-being-assessed-2026-04-08/">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Early in the morning, Iranian agencies report explosions from <a href="/wiki/Sirri_Island" title="Sirri Island">Sirri Island</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lavan_Island" title="Lavan Island">Lavan Island</a> of unknown origin. Iran accuses the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kuwait" title="Kuwait">Kuwait</a> of the attacks and launches retaliatory attacks against those countries in response. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.ynetnews.com/article/1cje8v7cv">(Ynet)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://wanaen.com/strikes-hit-lavan-refinery-iran-launches-retaliatory-attacks/">(Wanaen)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thailand</a> confirms the three crewmen on a vessel that was attacked in the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a> in March have died. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://aje.news/jf7llm?update=4473051">(Al Jazeera)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hezbollah%E2%80%93Israel_conflict_(2023%E2%80%93present)" title="Hezbollah–Israel conflict (2023–present)">Hezbollah–Israel conflict</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Lebanon_war" title="2026 Lebanon war">2026 Lebanon war</a>
<ul><li>Hundreds of people are killed and injured in a wave of <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> strikes on <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://aje.news/jf7llm?update=4473570">(Al Jazeera)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Politics and elections</b>
</p>
<ul><li>A pro-government protest is held in <a href="/wiki/Tehran" title="Tehran">Tehran</a> after the ceasefire is announced, with protesters chanting <a href="/wiki/Death_to_America" title="Death to America">Death to America</a>, <a href="/wiki/Death_to_Israel" title="Death to Israel">Death to Israel</a>, and death to compromisers. Protesters also burn the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_the_United_States" title="Flag of the United States">American</a> and <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Israel" title="Flag of Israel">Israeli</a> flags. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.business-standard.com/world-news/protesters-in-iran-express-outrage-at-us-israel-after-ceasefire-announced-126040800135_1.html">(<i>Business Standard</i>)</a></li></ul></div></div></div>
<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1305593205" /><div class="current-events"><div id="2026&#95;April&#95;07"></div>
<div role="region" aria-label="April 7" id="2026&#95;April&#95;7" class="current-events-main vevent">
    <div class="current-events-heading plainlinks">
        <div class="current-events-title" role="heading"><span class="summary">April&#160;7,&#160;2026<span style="display: none;">&#160;(<span class="bday dtstart published updated itvstart">2026-04-07</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span>
        </div>
        <ul class="current-events-navbar editlink noprint"><li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2026_April_7&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></li><li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2026_April_7&amp;action=history">history</a></li><li><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2026_April_7&amp;action=watch">watch</a></li>
        </ul>
    </div>
    <div class="current-events-content description">
<p><b>Armed conflicts and attacks</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Middle_Eastern_crisis_(2023%E2%80%93present)" title="Middle Eastern crisis (2023–present)">Middle Eastern crisis</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iran_war" title="2026 Iran war">2026 Iran war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2025%E2%80%932026_Iran%E2%80%93United_States_negotiations" title="2025–2026 Iran–United States negotiations">2025–2026 Iran–United States negotiations</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Islamabad_Accord_(2026)" class="mw-redirect" title="Islamabad Accord (2026)">Islamabad Accord</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">president</a> <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> announces on his <a href="/wiki/Truth_Social" title="Truth Social">Truth Social</a> that, based on conversations with <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Pakistan" title="Prime Minister of Pakistan">prime minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Shehbaz_Sharif" title="Shehbaz Sharif">Shehbaz Sharif</a> and <a href="/wiki/Field_marshal_(Pakistan)" title="Field marshal (Pakistan)">field marshal</a> <a href="/wiki/Asim_Munir" title="Asim Munir">Asim Munir</a>, he has agreed to "suspend the bombing and attacks on Iran for a period of two weeks", subject to Iran agreeing to the "complete, immediate and safe opening" of the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a>, and to allow time for an agreement to be reached. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.axios.com/2026/04/07/iran-2-week-ceasfire-trump-pakistan">(Axios)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_ambassadors_of_Iran_to_Pakistan" title="List of ambassadors of Iran to Pakistan">Iranian ambassador to Pakistan</a> <a href="/wiki/Reza_Amiri-Moghaddam" class="mw-redirect" title="Reza Amiri-Moghaddam">Reza Amiri-Moghaddam</a> says that the <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>-mediated framework aimed at a <a href="/wiki/Ceasefire" title="Ceasefire">ceasefire</a> to end the war has reached a "critical, sensitive stage". <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.wionews.com/photos/iran-envoy-to-pakistan-gives-update-on-negotiations-ahead-of-trump-s-tuesday-deadline-critical-stage-of-talks-war-to-end-big-power-plant-strike-1775546363320/1775546363321#goog_rewarded">(WIOnews)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://arynews.tv/pakistan-efforts-to-stop-war-critical-stage-iran-ambassador.amp">(ARY News)</a></li>
<li>Trump tells <a href="/wiki/Fox_News" title="Fox News">Fox News</a> that the U.S. is in "heated negotiations" with Iran after being briefed about the proposal. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.cbsnews.com/live-updates/iran-war-trump-deadline-power-plants-human-chains-israel-train-strikes/#post-update-1ce8735f">(CBS News)</a></li>
<li>It is reported that <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_United_States" title="Vice President of the United States">U.S. vice president</a> <a href="/wiki/JD_Vance" title="JD Vance">JD Vance</a> would serve as the U.S. <a href="/wiki/Interlocutor_(politics)" title="Interlocutor (politics)">interlocutor</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ceasefire" title="Ceasefire">ceasefire</a> talks. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.cbsnews.com/live-updates/iran-war-trump-deadline-power-plants-human-chains-israel-train-strikes/#post-update-62ba923d">(CBS News)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>Trump warns that "a whole <a href="/wiki/Iranian_civilization" class="mw-redirect" title="Iranian civilization">civilization</a> will die tonight" and will "never be brought back" if <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> does not agree to a deal by noon (<a href="/wiki/Greenwich_Mean_Time" title="Greenwich Mean Time">GMT</a>). <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/iran-us-israel-trump-lebanon-april-7-2026-421ee64fdc9a5c26460df8119c7d1b3f">(AP)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/trump-says-a-whole-civilization-will-die-tonight-if-iran-does-not-make-deal-2026-04-07/">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">The New York Times</a></i> reports that Iran has ended direct contact with the U.S. in response to Trump's latest threat to "end its civilization". However, <i><a href="/wiki/Tehran_Times" title="Tehran Times">Tehran Times</a></i> denies the reports by stating on <a href="/wiki/X_(social_network)" title="X (social network)">X</a> that "diplomatic and indirect channels of talks with US are not closed". <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aa.com.tr/en/middle-east/iran-cuts-direct-diplomacy-with-us-amid-rising-tensions-ahead-of-trumps-deadline/3896455">(AA)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.bloomberg.com/news/live-blog/2026-04-07/iran-latest-trump-hormuz-threats-deadline-middle-east-conflict-oil-markets">(Bloomberg)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.iranintl.com/en/202604077730?source=share-link">(Iran International)</a></li>
<li>Vance says that the war in Iran will conclude "very shortly", claiming that the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces" title="United States Armed Forces">U.S. military</a> has achieved all objectives. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.middleeastmonitor.com/20260407-iran-war-is-going-to-conclude-very-shortly-says-us-vice-president/">(Middle East Monitor)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2026_Strait_of_Hormuz_crisis" title="2026 Strait of Hormuz crisis">2026 Strait of Hormuz crisis</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> veto a <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_resolution" title="United Nations Security Council resolution">resolution</a> calling on <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_member_states" class="mw-redirect" title="United Nations member states">UN member states</a> to "coordinate efforts, defensive in nature" to ensure the safety of navigation in the Strait of Hormuz, saying that it was biased against Iran. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/4/7/russia-and-china-block-un-resolution-on-strait-of-hormuz">(Reuters via Al Jazeera)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iranian_strikes_on_Arab_countries" title="2026 Iranian strikes on Arab countries">2026 Iranian strikes on Arab countries</a>
<ul><li>Iran threatens to launch massive retaliatory strikes against the energy infrastructure <a href="/wiki/Energy_in_Saudi_Arabia" title="Energy in Saudi Arabia">of Saudi Arabia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Energy_in_the_United_Arab_Emirates" title="Energy in the United Arab Emirates">the UAE</a> in the event of a U.S. attack on its power plants. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.marketscreener.com/news/iran-s-tasnim-cites-military-source-as-saying-that-iran-will-add-oil-facilities-of-aramco-and-saudi-ce7e50dad989fe21">(MarketScreener)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.moneycontrol.com/world/iran-threatens-to-target-aramco-uae-pipelines-if-us-strikes-power-plants-report-article-13882909.html">(MoneyControl)</a></li>

<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a> is targeted by 12 <a href="/wiki/Ballistic_missile_program_of_Iran" title="Ballistic missile program of Iran">ballistic missiles</a>, two <a href="/wiki/Cruise_missile" title="Cruise missile">cruise missiles</a>, and 19 <a href="/wiki/Unmanned_aerial_vehicles_in_the_Iranian_military" title="Unmanned aerial vehicles in the Iranian military">drones</a> from <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://aje.news/ukui10?update=4466561">(Al Jazeera)</a></li></ul></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/2025%E2%80%932026_Iran%E2%80%93United_States_negotiations" title="2025–2026 Iran–United States negotiations">2025–2026 Iran–United States negotiations</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan_in_the_2026_Iran_war" title="Pakistan in the 2026 Iran war">Pakistan in the 2026 Iran war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> proposes a <a href="/wiki/Ceasefire" title="Ceasefire">ceasefire</a> plan received by <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, reportedly dubbed the <a href="/wiki/Islamabad_Accord_(2026)" class="mw-redirect" title="Islamabad Accord (2026)">Islamabad Accord</a>, which calls for an immediate halt to hostilities, the reopening of the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a>, and a 15–20 day period of negotiations between Iran and the U.S. This comes following reported talks between <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_the_Army_Staff_(Pakistan)" title="Chief of the Army Staff (Pakistan)">Pakistani army staff chief</a> <a href="/wiki/Asim_Munir" title="Asim Munir">Asim Munir</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_United_States" title="Vice President of the United States">U.S. vice president</a> <a href="/wiki/JD_Vance" title="JD Vance">JD Vance</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States_Special_Envoy" class="mw-redirect" title="United States Special Envoy">U.S. special envoy</a> <a href="/wiki/Steve_Witkoff" title="Steve Witkoff">Steve Witkoff</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Iran)" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Iran)">Iranian foreign minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Abbas_Araghchi" title="Abbas Araghchi">Abbas Araghchi</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Pakistan)" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Pakistan)">Pakistani foreign ministry</a> says that talks between Iran and the U.S. are ongoing. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.arabnews.com/node/2638953/amp">(<i>Arab News</i>)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/china/iran-us-receive-plan-end-hostilities-immediate-ceasefire-source-says-2026-04-06/">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">U.S. president</a> <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> says that Vance, Witkoff, and <a href="/wiki/Senior_Advisor_to_the_President_of_the_United_States" title="Senior Advisor to the President of the United States">senior presidential adviser</a> <a href="/wiki/Jared_Kushner" title="Jared Kushner">Jared Kushner</a> are talking to intermediaries in Pakistan on ending the war. He also calls the Iran proposal a "significant step" ahead of his Tuesday deadline. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aa.com.tr/en/us-israel-iran-war/trump-calls-iran-ceasefire-proposal-significant-step/3895131">(AA)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/trump-administration/live-blog/trump-defense-budget-gallego-taxes-congress-dhs-shutdown-live-updates-rcna266652/rcrd106900?canonicalCard=true">(NBC News)</a></li>
<li>Iran delivers its response to the United States via Pakistan, rejecting a temporary ceasefire and listing its own 10-point demands, which include a solution to all regional conflicts, lifting of <a href="/wiki/United_States_sanctions_against_Iran" title="United States sanctions against Iran">sanctions</a>, reconstruction, and a protocol to re-open the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2026/4/6/iran-war-live-tehran-rejects-trumps-tuesday-deadline-on-strait-of-hormuz">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.moneycontrol.com/world/iran-rejects-us-ceasefire-sends-a-tougher-10-point-end-war-plan-via-pakistan-article-13881513.html">(Moneycontrol)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Russo-Ukrainian_war_(2022%E2%80%93present)" title="Russo-Ukrainian war (2022–present)">Russo-Ukrainian war</a>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Cameroon" title="Cameroon">Cameroon</a> says Russia has confirmed that 16 <a href="/wiki/Cameroon_Armed_Forces" title="Cameroon Armed Forces">Cameroonian soldiers</a> have been killed in Ukraine while fighting alongside Russian forces. Cameroon's <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_foreign_affairs" title="Ministry of foreign affairs">foreign ministry</a> says "necessary arrangements" had been made to contact the families of the deceased soldiers. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/cameroon-soldiers-killed-russia-a2a3130018f378b73cc6167918b34b5d">(AP)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iranian_strikes_on_Bahrain" title="2026 Iranian strikes on Bahrain">2026 Iranian strikes on Bahrain</a>

An oil tank caught fire as a result. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.jpost.com/middle-east/article-892059">(<i>The Jerusalem Post</i>)</a></li></ul></li>

The <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Electricity,_Water_and_Renewable_Energy_(Kuwait)" title="Ministry of Electricity, Water and Renewable Energy (Kuwait)">electricity and water ministry</a> confirms the failure of two power generation units. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.thequint.com/news/breaking-news/iranian-drone-strikes-kuwait-oil-infrastructure-damage#read-more">(<i>The Quint</i>)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>

<li>At least four people are killed and 18 others are injured, including two children, when a passenger vehicle plunges off a road near Sojha in <a href="/wiki/Himachal_Pradesh" title="Himachal Pradesh">Himachal Pradesh</a>, <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/india/four-dead-after-passenger-vehicle-plunges-off-road-northern-india-ani-reports-2026-04-04/">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Three people are killed and at least 10 others are reportedly trapped after a four-story hotel collapses in <a href="/wiki/Anuppur" title="Anuppur">Anuppur</a>, <a href="/wiki/Madhya_Pradesh" title="Madhya Pradesh">Madhya Pradesh</a>, India. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.indiatoday.in/india/story/madhya-pradesh-four-storey-hotel-collapses-in-anuppur-kotma-several-feared-trapped-injured-2891643-2026-04-04">(<i>India Today</i>)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.hindustantimes.com/india-news/lodge-collapse-in-mps-anuppur-kills-three-so-far-several-feared-trapped-chilling-cctv-clip-shows-building-cave-in-101775377072684.html">(<i>Hindustan Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan_National_Disaster_Management_Authority" title="Afghanistan National Disaster Management Authority">Afghanistan National Disaster Management Authority</a> reports 77 deaths and 137 injuries in <a href="/wiki/Flood" title="Flood">flooding</a>, <a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">landslides</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lightning" title="Lightning">lightning</a> caused by <a href="/wiki/Severe_weather" title="Severe weather">severe weather</a> in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">the country</a> over the past 10 days. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/afghanistan-extreme-weather-flood-landslide-rain-storm-750d2cc1d9b4905a41e03c1cefbc1cf0">(AP)</a></li></ul>

This comes after protesters defy a previous order by the <a href="/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces" title="Israel Defense Forces">Israeli military</a> to limit gatherings to 150 people. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.haaretz.com/israel-news/israel-politics/2026-04-04/ty-article/.premium/idf-restricts-tel-aviv-anti-iran-war-protest-limits-turnout-to-150/0000019d-5805-d759-ab9d-799de33f0001">(Haaretz)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/police-clash-with-demonstrators-at-tel-aviv-anti-war-rally-despite-high-court-order-allowing-protests/">(<i>The Times of Israel</i>)</a></li></ul></li>

<p><b>Armed conflicts and attacks</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Middle_Eastern_crisis_(2023%E2%80%93present)" title="Middle Eastern crisis (2023–present)">Middle Eastern crisis</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iran_war" title="2026 Iran war">2026 Iran war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iranian_strikes_on_Arab_countries" title="2026 Iranian strikes on Arab countries">2026 Iranian strikes on Arab countries</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iranian_strikes_on_the_United_Arab_Emirates" title="2026 Iranian strikes on the United Arab Emirates">2026 Iranian strikes on the United Arab Emirates</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a> intercepts 18 <a href="/wiki/Ballistic_missile_program_of_Iran" title="Ballistic missile program of Iran">ballistic missiles</a>, four <a href="/wiki/Cruise_missile" title="Cruise missile">cruise missiles</a>, and 47 drones from <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>. Falling debris from the interception kills one person and injures others at the <a href="/wiki/Habshan" title="Habshan">Habshan</a> oil facility in the <a href="/wiki/Emirate_of_Abu_Dhabi" title="Emirate of Abu Dhabi">Abu Dhabi emirate</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/4/3/at-least-one-killed-at-uaes-habshan-gas-facility-after-intercepted-attack">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.vanguardngr.com/2026/04/12-injured-in-abu-dhabi-after-attack-intercepted/">(AFP via <i>Vanguard</i>)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2026_Strait_of_Hormuz_crisis" title="2026 Strait of Hormuz crisis">2026 Strait of Hormuz crisis</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Malta" title="Malta">Maltese</a>-flagged CMA CGM <i>Kribi</i>, a <a href="/wiki/Container_ship" title="Container ship">container ship</a> registered by <a href="/wiki/List_of_companies_of_France" title="List of companies of France">French</a> <a href="/wiki/Freight_transport" title="Freight transport">shipping</a> company <a href="/wiki/CMA_CGM" title="CMA CGM">CMA CGM</a> crosses the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a> after departing <a href="/wiki/Dubai" title="Dubai">Dubai</a>, making it the first ship from <a href="/wiki/Western_Europe" title="Western Europe">Western Europe</a> to cross the strait since the war started. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20260403-container-ship-declaring-french-ownership-passes-through-hormuz-strait">(AFP via France 24)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.euronews.com/business/2026/04/03/french-ship-crosses-strait-of-hormuz-in-first-western-european-transit-during-iran-war">(Euronews)</a></li>
<li>Japanese shipping company <a href="/wiki/Mitsui_O.S.K._Lines" title="Mitsui O.S.K. Lines">Mitsui O.S.K. Lines</a> says that a <a href="/wiki/Liquefied_natural_gas" title="Liquefied natural gas">liquefied natural gas</a> <a href="/wiki/Oil_tanker" title="Oil tanker">oil tanker</a> registered in <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> crosses the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a> for the first since the beginning of the Iran war. A third ship also crosses the strait. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://english.kyodonews.net/articles/-/73560">(Kyodo News)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2026/apr/03/french-owned-ship-japanese-tanker-pass-through-strait-of-hormuz-iran-war">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/List_of_aviation_shootdowns_and_accidents_during_the_2026_Iran_war" title="List of aviation shootdowns and accidents during the 2026 Iran war">Aviation shootdowns and accidents during the 2026 Iran war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Islamic_Republic_of_Iran_Armed_Forces" title="Islamic Republic of Iran Armed Forces">Iranian forces</a> shoot down a <a href="/wiki/United_States_Air_Force" title="United States Air Force">U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/McDonnell_Douglas_F-15E_Strike_Eagle" title="McDonnell Douglas F-15E Strike Eagle">F-15E</a> fighter jet in Iranian <a href="/wiki/Airspace" title="Airspace">airspace</a>. U.S. officials say a search is underway for the two crew members, one of whom, the pilot, is rescued. Iran's <a href="/wiki/State_media" title="State media">state media</a> says a reward will be given to any citizen who helps capture an American pilot. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://edition.cnn.com/2026/04/03/world/live-news/iran-war-us-trump-oil">(CNN)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/us-fighter-jet-shot-down-over-iran-search-underway-crew-us-official-says-2026-04-03/">(Reuters)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/2026/apr/03/us-fighter-jet-confirmed-shot-down-over-iran">(<i>The Guardian</i></a></li>

The pilot ejects and is rescued. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2026/apr/03/middle-east-crisis-live-trump-urges-iran-to-make-deal-after-bridge-strike?filterKeyEvents=false">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aa.com.tr/en/americas/2nd-us-air-force-combat-plane-crashes-in-persian-gulf-region-report/3891052">(AA)</a></li></ul></li>

<li>The <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Emergency_Situations_(Kyrgyzstan)" title="Ministry of Emergency Situations (Kyrgyzstan)">Kyrgyz emergency ministry</a> says that <a href="/wiki/Kyrgyzstan" title="Kyrgyzstan">Kyrgyzstan</a> has dispatched over 100 tons of humanitarian aid to Iran. The shipment is ordered by <a href="/wiki/President_of_Kyrgyzstan" title="President of Kyrgyzstan">Kyrgyz president</a> <a href="/wiki/Sadyr_Japarov" title="Sadyr Japarov">Sadyr Japarov</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://english.news.cn/20260403/212b1dcd499c4d55ab934ddb020648b3/c.html">(Xinhuanet)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2026_Lebanon_war" title="2026 Lebanon war">2026 Lebanon war</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Embassy_of_the_United_States,_Beirut" title="Embassy of the United States, Beirut">U.S. embassy</a> in <a href="/wiki/Beirut" title="Beirut">Beirut</a> warns Americans to leave <a href="/wiki/Lebanon" title="Lebanon">Lebanon</a> due to the situation in the country. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c93e9r62py4o">(BBC News)</a></li></ul></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2026_Afghanistan%E2%80%93Pakistan_conflict" title="2026 Afghanistan–Pakistan conflict">2026 Afghanistan–Pakistan conflict</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(China)" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs (China)">Chinese foreign ministry</a> spokesperson <a href="/wiki/Mao_Ning_(diplomat)" title="Mao Ning (diplomat)">Mao Ning</a> says that peace talks between <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> are advancing in an effort to end the war. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/pakistan-afghanistan-china-talks-fighting-urumqi-92f73bfacd2c6e68a4808ce8923b4645">(AP)</a></li></ul></li>

<ul><li>Six people are killed and five others, including a child, are injured in <a href="/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces" title="Russian Armed Forces">Russian</a> <a href="/wiki/Drone_warfare" title="Drone warfare">drone</a> and <a href="/wiki/Missile_strikes" class="mw-redirect" title="Missile strikes">missile strikes</a> across <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.dw.com/en/ukraine-kharkiv-under-repeated-attack-on-1500th-day-of-war/a-76652096">(DW)</a></li></ul></li></ul>

Min secures 429 votes, against 126 for <a href="/wiki/Nyo_Saw" title="Nyo Saw">Nyo Saw</a> and 29 for <a href="/wiki/Nan_Ni_Ni_Aye" title="Nan Ni Ni Aye">Nan Ni Ni Aye</a>, who become first and second <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_Myanmar" title="Vice President of Myanmar">vice presidents</a>, respectively. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://apnews.com/article/myanmar-president-min-aung-hlaing-military-c263b2d6175b82c5868e24496c975ff8">(AP)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://english.news.cn/20260403/3e711779db184062bfb35ba421604efb/c.html">(Xinhua)</a></li></ul></li>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iranian_strikes_on_Arab_countries" title="2026 Iranian strikes on Arab countries">2026 Iranian strikes on Arab countries</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Iranian_strikes_on_Bahrain" title="2026 Iranian strikes on Bahrain">2026 Iranian strikes on Bahrain</a>, <a href="/wiki/2026_Iranian_strikes_on_the_United_Arab_Emirates" title="2026 Iranian strikes on the United Arab Emirates">2026 Iranian strikes on the United Arab Emirates</a>
<ul><li>Minor damage is reported near the <a href="/wiki/Kizad" class="mw-redirect" title="Kizad">Kizad</a> area in <a href="/wiki/Abu_Dhabi" title="Abu Dhabi">Abu Dhabi</a> after the <a href="/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates" title="United Arab Emirates">United Arab Emirates</a> air defenses successfully intercepts an <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> missile. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.khaleejtimes.com/uae/damage-abu-dhabi-kezad-missile-interception">(<i>Khaleej Times</i>)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>Iran conducts strikes on <a href="/wiki/Amazon_Web_Services" title="Amazon Web Services">Amazon Web Services</a> servers in <a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a> and on an <a href="/wiki/Oracle_Corporation" title="Oracle Corporation">Oracle</a> data center in <a href="/wiki/Dubai" title="Dubai">Dubai</a>, United Arab Emirates. However, the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Dubai" title="Government of Dubai">Dubai government</a> dismisses any reports the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_Revolutionary_Guard_Corps" title="Islamic Revolutionary Guard Corps">Islamic Revolutionary Guard Corps</a> has targeted the Oracle data center and says it's false. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://caspianpost.com/iran/iran-s-irgc-targets-oracle-data-center-in-dubai">(<i>The Caspian Post</i>)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://gulfnews.com/uae/dubai-denies-reports-of-an-irgc-attack-on-an-oracle-data-centre-1.500494824">(<i>Gulf News</i>)</a></li></ul></li>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_(Iran)" title="Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Iran)">Iranian deputy foreign minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Kazem_Gharibabadi" title="Kazem Gharibabadi">Kazem Gharibabadi</a> says that Iran and <a href="/wiki/Oman" title="Oman">Oman</a> are drafting a protocol to oversee maritime transit through the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aa.com.tr/en/middle-east/iran-says-drafting-protocol-with-oman-to-oversee-strait-of-hormuz-transit/3889814">(AA)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> hosts a <a href="/wiki/Summit_(meeting)" title="Summit (meeting)">summit</a> with 40 countries to discuss reopening the <a href="/wiki/Strait_of_Hormuz" title="Strait of Hormuz">Strait of Hormuz</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/business/energy/dozens-countries-discuss-coalition-secure-passage-through-strait-hormuz-2026-04-02/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>

Eight people are killed and 95 others are injured. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/middle-easts-highest-bridge-linking-tehran-to-karaj-hit-by-airstrikes/">(Reuters via <i>The Times of Israel</i>)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://aje.news/1jg6hu?update=4457236">(Al Jazeera)</a></li></ul></li>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Kenya" title="Kenya">Kenya</a> reports at least 16 Kenyans are missing after being recruited to fight for the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces" title="Russian Armed Forces">Russian military</a> in <a href="/wiki/Ukraine" title="Ukraine">Ukraine</a>, while 38 others are currently in <a href="/wiki/List_of_hospitals_in_Russia" title="List of hospitals in Russia">Russian hospitals</a> in unknown conditions as they are under restricted access. <a href="/wiki/Prime_Cabinet_Secretary" title="Prime Cabinet Secretary">Prime Cabinet Secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/Musalia_Mudavadi" title="Musalia Mudavadi">Musalia Mudavadi</a> says the men were offered a <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">US$</a>2,700 monthly salary by Russian agents for joining the war. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/cx2ell79v2wo">(BBC News)</a></li></ul></li>

</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Economic_impact_of_the_2026_Iran_war" title="Economic impact of the 2026 Iran war">Economic impact of the 2026 Iran war</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Air_China" title="Air China">Air China</a>, <a href="/wiki/China_Southern_Airlines" title="China Southern Airlines">China Southern Airlines</a>, and its subsidiary <a href="/wiki/XiamenAir" title="XiamenAir">XiamenAir</a> increase <a href="/wiki/Fuel_surcharge" class="mw-redirect" title="Fuel surcharge">fuel surcharges</a> by <a href="/wiki/Renminbi" title="Renminbi">¥</a>60–120 (<a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">US$</a>8.70–17.50) on domestic flights in response to rising <a href="/wiki/Price_of_oil" title="Price of oil">oil prices</a> linked to the Iran war. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.thestandard.com.hk/world/article/328391/Chinese-airlines-to-raise-fuel-surcharges-on-domestic-flights">(AFP via <i>The Standard</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> increases fuel prices, raising <a href="/wiki/Petroleum_industry_in_Pakistan" title="Petroleum industry in Pakistan">petrol</a> by 42.7 percent and <a href="/wiki/Diesel_fuel" title="Diesel fuel">diesel</a> by 54.9 percent in response to higher global energy costs linked to the Iran war. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nst.com.my/world/world/2026/04/1409225/pakistan-hikes-petrol-diesel-prices-amid-mideast-war">(AFP via <i>New Straits Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Petroleum_in_the_United_States" title="Petroleum in the United States">crude oil</a> surges to over <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">$</a>113 per <a href="/wiki/Barrel_(unit)" title="Barrel (unit)">barrel</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.nbcnews.com/business/markets/oil-prices-stock-market-iran-war-trump-rcna266351">(NBC News)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Ports_(Somalia)" title="Ministry of Ports (Somalia)">Somali Ministry of Ports and Maritime Transport</a> announces that <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a> has registered the Guney (IMO 8230417) ship under the <a href="/wiki/Flag_of_Somalia" title="Flag of Somalia">Somali flag</a>, its first national-flagged vessel since 1991. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.ftlsomalia.com/somalia-launches-first-national-ship-registry-since-1991/">(FTL Somalia)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aa.com.tr/en/africa/somalia-registers-ship-under-national-flag-after-over-3-decades/3888956">(Anadolu Ajansı)</a></li></ul>
<p><b>Disasters and accidents</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_North_Maluku_earthquake" title="2026 North Maluku earthquake">2026 North Maluku earthquake</a>
<ul><li>One person is killed and another is injured when a building in <a href="/wiki/Manado" title="Manado">Manado</a>, <a href="/wiki/North_Sulawesi" title="North Sulawesi">North Sulawesi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>, collapses following a 7.4-magnitude earthquake that struck <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Indonesia" title="Eastern Indonesia">eastern Indonesia</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20260402-7-4-magnitude-quake-off-indonesia-kills-one-tsunami-warning-lifted">(AFP via France 24)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2025%E2%80%9326_European_windstorm_season" title="2025–26 European windstorm season">2025–26 European windstorm season</a>
<ul><li>One person is killed and hundreds are trapped indoors by <a href="/wiki/Flooding" class="mw-redirect" title="Flooding">flooding</a> in <a href="/wiki/Nea_Makri" title="Nea Makri">Nea Makri</a>, <a href="/wiki/Attica_(region)" title="Attica (region)">Attica</a>, <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greece</a>, amid <a href="/wiki/Gale" title="Gale">gale</a>-force winds along the <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_coast" class="mw-redirect" title="Mediterranean coast">Mediterranean coast</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/sustainability/climate-energy/storm-batters-greece-killing-one-flooding-homes-disrupting-travel-2026-04-02/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>Four people are killed when a <a href="/wiki/Cessna_172" title="Cessna 172">Cessna 172</a> crashes into a field in <a href="/wiki/Huejotzingo" title="Huejotzingo">Huejotzingo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Puebla" title="Puebla">Puebla</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://potosinoticias.com/2026/04/02/aeronave-se-estrella-en-huejotzingo-puebla-al-menos-4-personas-murieron/">(PotosíNoticias <small>in Spanish</small>)</a></li>
<li>Both pilots are killed when a <a href="/wiki/Beechcraft_Model_18" title="Beechcraft Model 18">Beechcraft Model 18</a> operating on a cargo flight crashes in <a href="/wiki/Coron,_Palawan" title="Coron, Palawan">Coron</a>, <a href="/wiki/Palawan" title="Palawan">Palawan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://english.news.cn/20260402/14ec201f5c1a4f61b8ee03b4f694effe/c.html">(Xinhua)</a></li></ul>
<p><b>International relations</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Argentina%E2%80%93Iran_relations" title="Argentina–Iran relations">Argentina–Iran relations</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a> orders <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iranian</a> <a href="/wiki/Charg%C3%A9_d%27affaires" title="Chargé d&#39;affaires">chargé d'affaires</a> Mohsen Soltani Tehrani to leave the country within 48 hours after Iranian officials issued statements that Argentina described as false and offensive. The move follows Argentina's designation of the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_Revolutionary_Guard_Corps" title="Islamic Revolutionary Guard Corps">Islamic Revolutionary Guard Corps</a> as a <a href="/wiki/Terrorism_in_Argentina" title="Terrorism in Argentina">terrorist</a> organization. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.lbcgroup.tv/news/world-news/920881/argentina-expels-irans-diplomatic-envoy/en">(AFP via LBCI)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Moldova%E2%80%93Russia_relations" title="Moldova–Russia relations">Moldova–Russia relations</a>, <a href="/wiki/Accession_of_Moldova_to_the_European_Union" title="Accession of Moldova to the European Union">Accession of Moldova to the European Union</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Moldova" title="Moldova">Moldova</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Moldova" title="Parliament of Moldova">parliament</a> approves the country's withdrawal from the <a href="/wiki/Commonwealth_of_Independent_States" title="Commonwealth of Independent States">Commonwealth of Independent States</a> (CIS), as <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Moldova" title="Government of Moldova">the government</a> says CIS's core values and  principles are no longer respected, such as territorial integrity and the inviolability of borders, and refers to Russia's actions in the region, including the <a href="/wiki/Russo-Ukrainian_war" title="Russo-Ukrainian war">war against Ukraine</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Operational_Group_of_Russian_Forces" title="Operational Group of Russian Forces">illegal military presence on Moldovan territory</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.moldpres.md/eng/politics/parliament-votes-for-moldova-s-final-withdrawal-from-the-cis">(Moldova Press)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://tass.com/world/2110711">(TASS)</a></li></ul></li></ul>
<p><b>Law and crime</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2025_Drents_Museum_heist" title="2025 Drents Museum heist">2025 Drents Museum heist</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Dutch</a> authorities recover the <a href="/wiki/Helmet_of_Co%C8%9Bofene%C8%99ti" title="Helmet of Coțofenești">Helmet of Coțofenești</a> and other treasures from the <a href="/wiki/Dacians" title="Dacians">Dacian</a> royal collection, which were stolen from the <a href="/wiki/Drents_Museum" title="Drents Museum">Drents Museum</a> in <a href="/wiki/Assen" title="Assen">Assen</a>, <a href="/wiki/Drenthe" title="Drenthe">Drenthe</a>, in 2025. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/article/stolen-romanian-golden-helmet-found-dutch-art-sleuth-to-afp/">(AFP via CTV News)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kampala_school_stabbing" title="Kampala school stabbing">Kampala school stabbing</a>
<ul><li>Four children are killed in a <a href="/wiki/Mass_stabbing" title="Mass stabbing">mass stabbing</a> at a school in <a href="/wiki/Kampala" title="Kampala">Kampala</a>, <a href="/wiki/Uganda" title="Uganda">Uganda</a>. The suspected perpetrator, an adult man, is arrested. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2026/4/2/four-children-killed-in-school-stabbing-attack-in-uganda">(Al Jazeera)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Opposition_to_Vladimir_Putin_in_Russia" title="Opposition to Vladimir Putin in Russia">Opposition to Vladimir Putin in Russia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Protests_against_the_Russo-Ukrainian_war_(2022%E2%80%93present)" title="Protests against the Russo-Ukrainian war (2022–present)">Protests against the Russo-Ukrainian war</a>
<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Basmanny_District_Court" title="Basmanny District Court">Basmanny District Court</a> in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, sentences <a href="/wiki/Germans" title="Germans">German</a> sculptor <a href="/wiki/Jacques_Tilly" title="Jacques Tilly">Jacques Tilly</a> <a href="/wiki/Trial_in_absentia" title="Trial in absentia">in absentia</a> to eight years and six months in <a href="/wiki/Prisons_in_Russia" title="Prisons in Russia">prison</a> for spreading <a href="/wiki/Disinformation_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine" title="Disinformation in the Russian invasion of Ukraine">false information</a> about <a href="/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces" title="Russian Armed Forces">the military</a> and offending <a href="/wiki/Religion_in_Russia" title="Religion in Russia">religious believers</a> through his public works and statements concerning <a href="/wiki/Russo-Ukrainian_war_(2022%E2%80%93present)" title="Russo-Ukrainian war (2022–present)">Russia's actions in Ukraine</a>. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/russian-court-convicts-german-sculptor-absentia-depicting-putin-patriarch-sex-2026-04-02/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>Twelve people are injured when a masked man detonates two <a href="/wiki/Pyrotechnics" title="Pyrotechnics">pyrotechnic</a> explosives on an train in <a href="/wiki/Siegburg" title="Siegburg">Siegburg</a>, <a href="/wiki/North_Rhine-Westphalia" title="North Rhine-Westphalia">North Rhine-Westphalia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>. A 20-year-old man is arrested by <a href="/wiki/Federal_Police_(Germany)" title="Federal Police (Germany)">Federal Police</a> and charged with attempted murder, aggravated assault, and violation of explosives law. A right-wing political motive is suspected. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.deutschlandfunk.de/anschlagsdrohung-in-ice-verdaechtiger-in-u-haft-100.html">(Deutschlandfunk)</a></li></ul>
<p><b>Politics and elections</b>
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/2026_Cuban_crisis" title="2026 Cuban crisis">2026 Cuban crisis</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a> announces the pardon of 2,010 prisoners, with releases scheduled over the coming months based on criteria such as conduct and health. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.freemalaysiatoday.com/category/world/2026/04/03/cuba-pardons-2010-prisoners-in-humanitarian-easter-gesture">(AFP via <i>Free Malaysia Today</i>)</a></li></ul></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Second_cabinet_of_Donald_Trump" title="Second cabinet of Donald Trump">Second cabinet of Donald Trump</a>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">U.S. president</a> <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> dismisses <a href="/wiki/Pam_Bondi" title="Pam Bondi">Pam Bondi</a> as <a href="/wiki/United_States_Attorney_General" title="United States Attorney General">Attorney General</a>, with <a href="/wiki/United_States_Deputy_Attorney_General" title="United States Deputy Attorney General">Deputy Attorney General</a> <a href="/wiki/Todd_Blanche" title="Todd Blanche">Todd Blanche</a> replacing her on an acting basis. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/ce843ge47z4o">(BBC News)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.cnn.com/2026/04/02/politics/pam-bondi-role-trump">(CNN)</a></li></ul></li>
<li>General <a href="/wiki/Randy_George" title="Randy George">Randy George</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chief_of_Staff_of_the_United_States_Army" title="Chief of Staff of the United States Army">Chief of Staff of the United States Army</a>, steps down upon <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_Defense" title="United States Secretary of Defense">U.S. defense secretary</a> <a href="/wiki/Pete_Hegseth" title="Pete Hegseth">Pete Hegseth</a>'s request. <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.cbsnews.com/news/hegseth-ousts-army-chief-of-staff-gen-randy-george/">(CBS News)</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.reuters.com/world/us/hegseth-has-asked-us-army-chief-staff-step-down-cbs-news-reports-2026-04-02/">(Reuters)</a></li></ul></div></div></div>

<div role="region" aria-labelledby="Elections&#95;and&#95;referenda" class="mw-collapsible current-events-sidebar" style="width:30em">
<div><div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Elections_and_referendums"><a href="/wiki/2026_national_electoral_calendar" title="2026 national electoral calendar">Elections and referendums</a></h2></div></div>
<div class="mw-collapsible-content">
<dl><dd><div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Recent">Recent</h3></div></dd></dl>
